  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f3e0549a-5331-46c1-b4a1-f1c078d6ce08'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText2352188202008185815" style="display:none">Breathe in. Breathe out. This mantra gets Tessa Benson through the day. <br /> <br />The man she loves walks all over her, and she just wants to get by without her heart shattering to pieces. And the person who paid to watch her die...is still out there somewhere. <br /> <br />Tessa prowls dark neighborhoods in a quest for justice, but she doesn’t find the killer. Not until they strike again…in the place Tessa is least expecting, and where it hurts worst.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8900884408793646427">Warning. This book contains some major triggers. It contains violence, sexual assault, and scenes of PTSD. <br/><br/>Tessa has a complicated love life. The man she likes, Tom, wants nothing to do with her. The man who likes her, Gerald, she wants nothing to do with. To unwind from her troubled life, Tessa goes out with a friend. What started as a fun night ends up in violent despair. Tessa is taken by two men, kidnapped and held hostage in a lone cabin. They videotape the mental and physical torture she e</span>
  <span id="freeText8900884408793646427" style="display:none">Warning. This book contains some major triggers. It contains violence, sexual assault, and scenes of PTSD. <br /><br />Tessa has a complicated love life. The man she likes, Tom, wants nothing to do with her. The man who likes her, Gerald, she wants nothing to do with. To unwind from her troubled life, Tessa goes out with a friend. What started as a fun night ends up in violent despair. Tessa is taken by two men, kidnapped and held hostage in a lone cabin. They videotape the mental and physical torture she experiences. Sure that she will not make it out alive, Tessa fights back and escapes. Yet the pain of her experience lingers—she suffers from serious PTSD, often turning violent herself. Determined to find out who orchestrated the kidnapping, Tessa and a cop Tobin, whom she begins to develop feelings for, seek out answers.<br /><br />Breathe In is definitely not a novel for the faint of heart. Tessa endures things that take her to the very brink of a dangerous edge. It was hard to read what her kidnappers put it through. The process of her grief and anger was realistic and heartbreaking. The inner psychology of being the survivor of extreme abuse is well written and very emotional. It is hard not to feel for Tessa. And her anger? You don’t dislike her for what she does because you sympathize and understand her pain. The end came as a surprise, and the victory much needed. I can’t say she that her pain was assuaged, but the cathartic revenge at the end was enough to satisfy the need for resolution.<br /></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_2903870023" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2903870023" />
    <a title="Jewel Hart" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart"><img alt="Jewel Hart" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595707974p2/56470711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2903870023?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jewel Hart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jewel Hart" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart">Jewel Hart</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2903870023" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14535802459790747674">Breathe In by award winning author, Michelle Bellon is a riveting story of one woman’s terrifying account of her kidnapping, torture and the vengeance she seeks. It is a must read, dark and thrilling story subjecting the reader to breathless anticipation while on the edge of their seat from beginning to end.<br/><br/>Tessa Benson’s love life is difficult and not so great. Sick of the relationships with the men in her life, vulnerable and struggling to find a voice of her own, Tessa decides to take a breat</span>
  <span id="freeText14535802459790747674" style="display:none">Breathe In by award winning author, Michelle Bellon is a riveting story of one woman’s terrifying account of her kidnapping, torture and the vengeance she seeks. It is a must read, dark and thrilling story subjecting the reader to breathless anticipation while on the edge of their seat from beginning to end.<br /><br />Tessa Benson’s love life is difficult and not so great. Sick of the relationships with the men in her life, vulnerable and struggling to find a voice of her own, Tessa decides to take a breather from her conflicted life and heads out for the night with a friend. What she had anticipated would be a fun night out to forget her troubles, turns into the worst nightmare she could ever have imagined. She is kidnapped, tortured and held captive. Her captor’s video tape the entire ordeal. Terrified her life is about to end, she puts up a fight and manages to escape. Tessa is now filled with mental and emotional pain, extreme anger and agonizes with PTSD. Determined to discover who is behind her kidnapping and find answers, she gets help from Tobin, an understanding policeman, who she connects with and begins to have feelings for.<br /><br />Breathe In by Michelle Bellon is a dark, thrilling page-turner filled with suspense, twists and turns and scenes that are terrifying and nightmarish in nature. The potential suspects kept me guessing and very intrigued, which made this book skillfully written with a unique voice, well-conceived effective storyline and dynamic plot. Although this is an original piece of fiction, it does happen in real life, making it that much more of a realistic, intense and chilling story. The fact that the kidnapper’s video tapped the torture and probable death of Tessa, will have the reader thinking of all the sickos out there who get off on watching such snuff films. Despite the dark content of this book, author, Michelle Bellon draws the reader in with the clever mystery of the plot and the intensity of the emotions, actions and personalities of the characters. I loved how Tessa evolved into a strong woman who developed her own voice despite her toxic relationships, and devastating, life-altering events. The resulting violent tendencies she began to display (no matter how severe or wrong), I felt, were totally justified and actually, I would have, most likely, done the same thing. This exceedingly interesting book is thought-provoking and will engage the reader on so many levels. Breathe In by Michelle Bellon is compelling, engrossing and gripping with a fast-paced narrative, strong original plot, well developed realistic and likable characters who readers will fully connect with and be pulling for throughout. The ending is completely gratifying, pleasing readers that vengeance prevailed.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14535802459790747674" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2107210970" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7974140605667238703">I received an arc through a group that normally offers romance based books, so a straight up thriller is not a genre I typically read. Hence, this is one heck of a book to have impressed and captivated me in the way that it did. I'd planned on reading it over a couple of days, but ended up reading late into the night (ok early hours!) to complete it.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1502729064p8/3612309.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Tessa <i>can</i> be annoying at times, but it makes her very human and real. She starts out as a doormat, allowing herself to be treated badly by others. I</span>
  <span id="freeText7974140605667238703" style="display:none">I received an arc through a group that normally offers romance based books, so a straight up thriller is not a genre I typically read. Hence, this is one heck of a book to have impressed and captivated me in the way that it did. I'd planned on reading it over a couple of days, but ended up reading late into the night (ok early hours!) to complete it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1502729064p8/3612309.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tessa <i>can</i> be annoying at times, but it makes her very human and real. She starts out as a doormat, allowing herself to be treated badly by others. I loved how she found her voice and her inner strength, as she comes to terms with her ordeal, and became that phoenix.<br><br>The book does feel a little slow at first, but that could have been because I was waiting for her to be kidnapped. Because of that the suspense and angst kicked off from the start for me! Kidnappers aside there are 3 male characters and, for me, they <b>
  <i>all</i>
</b> became suspects, either on their own or in some combination, at different points in the book. <b>That</b> is the quality of the writing.<br><br>The plot is never confusing but various facts/observations emerge that turn your thoughts first one way, then the other. The kidnap scenes are dark and contain a lot of potential triggers. Tessa's reactions and feelings after the kidnap felt so very <i>real</i> and whilst some of her actions were criminal (and in a big way), you sort of couldn't blame her. <br><br>Some reviewers have mentioned about the romance in this book. As an avid romance reader, I personally found the romance very vague and minimal, but it isn't what the book is about so I was OK with that. <br><br>Whilst there is a very <i>
  <b>definite</b>
</i> conclusion to the story, I didn't know where life was heading for Tessa. Would she continue her vigilante ways? Did she intend on commencing a relationship with Tobin? And the biggest was over the delivery of the SD card - for me that was the only unrealistic part of the book. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Unless it was Tessa, but then later in the scene it suggested she was with Tobin and I can't see that he would have allowed that action. And surely the police would have gone to both locations at the same time? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>I've not read any work by this author before, but I will be keeping an eye out for her work in future.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText7046290724614810824" style="display:none">"We don't always get to choose who we want to be initially. But it seems, if we're lucky, we eventually get the opportunity to choose who we want to be in the end."<br /><br />5 Stars!<br /><br />WHAT A BOOK!!!!<br />This book was way more than I expected.<br />This book was raw and emotional. It didn't try to coverup or sugar coat anything.<br />Tessa is just a normal woman. She keeps to herself most of the time. She doesn't bother anymore.<br />After getting out of a short relationship, she feels lost.<br />One night she is kidnapped by two men. She is taken to a cabin in the woods and held there. Her time there is terrible but luckily she manages to escape.<br />With the person behind her kidnapping still out there, she doesn't know who to trust.<br />When she makes friends with the officer working her case, Officer MacGregor, her life starts to change. She starts to believe in her self more.<br />She is not the timid, shy girl she used to be. She lost that when she was kidnapped.<br />But what happens when she gets overwhelmed?<br />What happens when it gets to much to handle?<br />Will Tessa be able to handle the pain and the PTSD or will she give into them?<br />What happens when Tessa decides to take the law into her own hands? Will she survive?<br />You have to read to find out!<br /> <br />WOW!!!!! <br /><br />What a story. This is the first time I have read this author and I will defiantly read more of her books.<br />Tessa lived thought a terrible event. But even when she escaped, the torment wasn't over. This book shows that even if you look okay on the outside, sometimes the inside is screaming for help. Tessa endures a lot in this book and it takes a toll on her body, both physically and mentally.<br />There were parts of this book that were hard to read, but without them, the story would not have ben what it is. This is defiantly a 5 star book for me.<br /><br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Pierson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Pierson" href="/user/show/18244539-jennifer-pierson">Jennifer Pierson</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2107714140" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4542282830460205246">This is the first book that I've read by this author, and the original page turner kept me on the edge of my seat cover to cover. Tessa Benson has been used as a doormat by the men in her life lately, and all she wants to do is get by with her heart intact. That all changes the day that she gets kidnapped, where she wakes up tied to a filthy bed with a camera recording every minute. And while she's getting tortured, something in her breaks, and she escapes with her life. Now she's done with peop</span>
  <span id="freeText4542282830460205246" style="display:none">This is the first book that I've read by this author, and the original page turner kept me on the edge of my seat cover to cover. Tessa Benson has been used as a doormat by the men in her life lately, and all she wants to do is get by with her heart intact. That all changes the day that she gets kidnapped, where she wakes up tied to a filthy bed with a camera recording every minute. And while she's getting tortured, something in her breaks, and she escapes with her life. Now she's done with people walking all over her, being scared, and the injustices of the world. As she gets stronger, the people who had to do with her abduction are still out there, and this time they strike where it really hurts her. This was a crazy, dark read that fed my inner dark &amp; twisty self quite well. At first, Tessa really irritated me, but after she escapes on her own, the bad a** that she became, had me cheering on the sidelines the rest of the way in. Michelle Bellon's super talented writing style was so intense, that all of Tessa's feelings of hurt, helplessness, and finally anger, permeated the air all around me, as they seeped out of my kindle, to where I physically felt all of them. Diabolical twists &amp; turns turned my room into a symphony of colorful metaphors, and I'm still dropping a few f-bombs. Now I have one big issue with this intense read, and remember this is only MY OPINION, but important to me, the ending just dropped off for me. I needed so much more after her powerfully moving journey. With all of that being said, I HIGHLY RECOMMEND! </span>
  <a data-text-id="4542282830460205246" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8757292303754518022">Thanks to Reading Deals for a copy to read and review.<br/><br/> I admire the way this author wrote but it's a fence book as far as a dark read. The following is my opinion of the book and it may contain spoilers that will reduce your reading pleasure.<br/> Tessa is the main character, the book starts out awkward because she is literally standing outside the door of a man she has been dating. Only he hasn't replied to her texts, nor has he ever invited her to his house. Warning signs anyone? When he does answe</span>
  <span id="freeText8757292303754518022" style="display:none">Thanks to Reading Deals for a copy to read and review.<br /><br /> I admire the way this author wrote but it's a fence book as far as a dark read. The following is my opinion of the book and it may contain spoilers that will reduce your reading pleasure.<br /> Tessa is the main character, the book starts out awkward because she is literally standing outside the door of a man she has been dating. Only he hasn't replied to her texts, nor has he ever invited her to his house. Warning signs anyone? When he does answer the door, not only is he an jerk but I really don't see what she sees in him. Then on the way back to her apartment she runs into another guy...Gerald, who she doesn't really like but she dated him. She doesn't know how to tell him she's not interested. <br /> First of all Tessa appears weak, not only because of Tom but because she can't tell Gerald to go suck himself. If your not interested just say so. Although Tessa goes through a harrowing ordeal she kills her attackers which some might say is closure. She doesn't stop killing there, which I find weird...that can't be normal. I say she went psycho...I mean who commits murder in self defense and then goes out and commits premeditated murder.....uh Tessa. Then the author acts like she is going to have Tessa fight another husband from her violence abuse group but it kind of drops off. Ending had merit but I was looking for her to not let Tom off the hook. So fence book....three stars for entertainment.</span>

  <span id="freeText10158792896891027227" style="display:none">This is my first book by Michelle Bellon. I absolutely loved it! I was unsure what to expect when I picked up this book. The story told surpassed my any expectation I may have had. I don't really want to give anything away. I will say the story was extremely well written. I really enjoyed each character and what they brought to the book. I'm giving 4.5 stars because I truly enjoyed this book but I had a couple of left when the book was over. Why was Tessa so frightened and clingy in the beginning in the first part of the story? Why the hate from the Librarian boos lady? It was just a few things I was curious about. I would have liked more background on a few of the characters. I loved Tessa’s growth after her kidnapping. I loved the show of her very real struggle to come to terms with what happened to her; trying to find out who she is now, how to live again and where her life is now going. I'm loving that the author made this very real for me while reading. I figured out the whole who dunnit pretty early on in the story and was eagerly reading to see how it would be handled. I loved the way it was written when Tessa finds out who did everything. This story for me was a wonderful story of survival and hope. I definitely recommend this book to anyone who loves a good book about about surviving against all odds, hope, and claiming your place in this world no matter what.<br /><br />**received an advanced copy for an honest review **</span>

<div id="review_2659823803" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2659823803" />
    <a title="Maria Logan-Montgomery" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66219901-maria-logan-montgomery"><img alt="Maria Logan-Montgomery" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546387948p2/66219901.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2659823803?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria Logan-Montgomery" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria Logan-Montgomery" href="/user/show/66219901-maria-logan-montgomery">Maria Logan-Montgomery</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2659823803" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13547210518455888826">Tessa Benson is a Ph.D. librarian – smart and well-educated. Still, she falls victim to human sexual trafficking. How could this happen to such a smart person? Answer: it can happen to anyone.<br/><br/>In her award-winning book, Breathe In, Michelle Bellon explores not only human trafficking, but the importance of self-confidence in women, as well as the importance of being careful of who you date. In other words, if he treats you badly, walk away and don’t look back.<br/><br/>“Breathe In, breathe out” is a mantra </span>
  <span id="freeText13547210518455888826" style="display:none">Tessa Benson is a Ph.D. librarian – smart and well-educated. Still, she falls victim to human sexual trafficking. How could this happen to such a smart person? Answer: it can happen to anyone.<br /><br />In her award-winning book, Breathe In, Michelle Bellon explores not only human trafficking, but the importance of self-confidence in women, as well as the importance of being careful of who you date. In other words, if he treats you badly, walk away and don’t look back.<br /><br />“Breathe In, breathe out” is a mantra taught to the timid Tessa by her therapist, and she uses it for any stressful situation. The description of Tessa’s treatment by her captors was graphic, and disgusting, but in order to be true to the reality of these crimes, it was necessary. The book is well-written, and flows smoothly. After the action began, I couldn’t put it down. I was glad to see a timid woman morph into a strong, angry female character who could not only fight back, but also stand up for herself and others.<br /><br />For me, the identity of the bad guy was obvious almost immediately. He was making money, big money, in a way I had no idea existed – filming the abuse and murder of girls and women, then selling the videos. The thought that this actually happens is truly frightening. I thank Ms. Bellon for educating us about this atrocity with Breathe In. I will definitely be reading the work of this author again.<br /><br />What Makes This Reviewer Grumpy?<br /><br />I expected poor grammar on the part of Tessa’s probably uneducated captors. However, poor grammar on the part of a character with a Ph.D., as well as the voice of the narrator is unacceptable:<br />“I wish I wouldn’t have…” instead of I” wish I hadn’t…” and “where it’s at…” instead of “where it is…”; redundancies such as “contemplate over” instead of simply “contemplate”; and of course, the all too common mistakes of confusing further and farther; split infinitives, and missing commas.<br />Look for me online as The Grumpy Book Reviewer.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13547210518455888826" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText4630904594871658885" style="display:none">Tessa was just an ordinary woman, meek and mild and a little bit of a push over, particularly when it comes to the man in her life. That is until she learns how dark others can truly be, as well as finding the darkness in herself, as a cooping mechanism after surviving a brutal torture and kidnap, Never meant to survive she finds a way to escape, but the pain is far from over. Suffering from severe post traumatic stress disorder and without an outlet for her pain she turns to vigilantism, hoping to find the men that hurt her. With the help of sympathetic policeman Tobin, will she find the answers she is looking for, how will she feel once the truth is finally revealed? <br /><br />Twisted, grisly and unflinching, this 'Breathe In' by Michelle Bellon takes on some difficult themes including PTSD, sexual assault, and graphic violence, but the author handles them really well. The novel is exciting, shocking and although you are presented with a number of suspects throughout, the ending is sure to surprise you. A 5 star thriller.<br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2392292379" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6937548225491601463">Breathe In is a captivating crime novel that it really well-written, with a plot that keeps the reader guessing right up until the revelation in the final few chapters. Michelle Bellon expertly crafts a thriller that sees her complicated protagonist Tessa hell bent on revenge against the two men who brutalise her and in doing so, risks going somewhere that she can never come back from.<br/><br/>I really felt for Tessa, the ultimate pain and grief she felt following the attack was set to devour her complet</span>
  <span id="freeText6937548225491601463" style="display:none">Breathe In is a captivating crime novel that it really well-written, with a plot that keeps the reader guessing right up until the revelation in the final few chapters. Michelle Bellon expertly crafts a thriller that sees her complicated protagonist Tessa hell bent on revenge against the two men who brutalise her and in doing so, risks going somewhere that she can never come back from.<br /><br />I really felt for Tessa, the ultimate pain and grief she felt following the attack was set to devour her completely. Revenge seemed to be the only way she could find her way out, and it does make you wonder how you yourself would react after such an awful violation. Her reaction may seem extreme but she is someone who has been taken advantage of her whole life, looking for justice is a way of ending that chapter of her life once and for all. I really enjoyed this book, the plot was full of surprises and I kept changing my mind on who the culprits were. The conclusion was thrilling and not at all disappointing, I will be looking for more from Michelle Bellon in the future.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5996160572599165918">Guardians of Eastgate: Book One of the Seer Series by Sherry Leclerc is a great fantasy book with a wealth of mystical creatures. With a map in the beginning of the book that details the lands that these creatures live in, the author sets the tone well, and gives the reader this added bit of information in order to fully enjoy the story. The names of the characters are particularly beautiful, from Maelona to Kelwyn and add to the beautiful sense of the story. Of course there is an ancient evil t</span>
  <span id="freeText5996160572599165918" style="display:none">Guardians of Eastgate: Book One of the Seer Series by Sherry Leclerc is a great fantasy book with a wealth of mystical creatures. With a map in the beginning of the book that details the lands that these creatures live in, the author sets the tone well, and gives the reader this added bit of information in order to fully enjoy the story. The names of the characters are particularly beautiful, from Maelona to Kelwyn and add to the beautiful sense of the story. Of course there is an ancient evil that must be fought and conquered , that being a rather classic way of putting together a fantasy tale. Beyond that, there are undercurrents that suggest that one learn self acceptance, and perhaps this is the biggest overall moral lesson to the story. A bit of romance and mystery add balance to the tale, while the dialogue and character development is spot on. Highly recommend for an engaging book that allows the reader to escape for a while.</span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6K66LYTgmPCatXDlbPPQy9fb5JT/YAM1Vlm/A1Q49a70lDjzWAn9oTPgbr89JPV2xn479cf1U8+pMh+OXH4sbA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nPxLk1KMfkSIZBFy4Afi4aiXcBHuiyXL/x3LJRt3Eu6AxslNjmUbFSExDyix0MdcuTKvcNYedTEAdmuoEzHLLA==')})
  }
//]]>

The book is scheduled for release on the 1st of October. As a Business Strategy and Psychological Warfare Consultant, M.D. White wrote this book utilizing his countless experiences over the years to properly proffer working, tested and trusted strategies to help business owners or employees, business managers or executives, politicians and or public figures manage high-stake business and leadership situations with the greatest success. White had this to say: &quot;No amount of experience in crucial conversations, or business negotiations, can prepare you better than the information you\'ll gleam from this manual. It\'s truly a politician’s guide to psychological warfare. Perhaps its President Trumps bible, and what he reads everynight. The moral of the story is: Use it, or be used by it! Current geopolitical controversies only emphasize this point.&quot; Many have deliberated over the effect of military strategies in business, but M.D. White cuts to the chase and reveals the raw and missing pieces all other military strategy discussions have left out. In this book, White extracts the key ingredients of military strategies and the applications which are left out in most discussions. For the first time ever there is a clear work-around of military strategies and an easy to understand roadmap on learning how to unlock, grow and strengthen from within one’s influence, presence and abilities. The Author further stressed the effectiveness of military strategies in business. “This military-based guide to business takes the best wartime tactics and practices and teaches you how you can apply them in your business—and your political or personal life—successfully. Developed within a systematic and comprehensive framework, this book utilizes the art of war in a whole new way and reveals that the path to a smooth business victory and mutually beneficial dialogue can be found in an unexpected but rewarding place.”  The world of business is a battlefield. You must be prepared.  Sun Tzu said, “The art of war teaches us to rely not on the likelihood of the enemy’s not coming, but on our own readiness to receive him.” The takeaway? Do everything in your power to be prepared, because it\'s only a matter of time before something goes wrong. If you are running, founding, working in any business, or are in an environment where ‘politics’ yield to nobody, The Influence of Military Strategies to Business is the preparation you need to succeed.
